    <script type="application/ld+json">{"@context":"https://schema.org","@type":"DiscussionForumPosting","headline":"Use-after-free in `zoneinfo.get_weak_cache` via weak DECREF assumption","articleBody":"### What happened?\n\n`get_weak_cache()` assumes that `_weak_cache` is always owned by the object and safe to DECREF. When _weak_cache is a descriptor returning a new object, this assumption breaks, causing the cache object to be freed too early and leading to a use-after-free in `zoneinfo_ZoneInfo_impl()`.\n\n**Proof of Concept:**\n```python\nfrom zoneinfo import ZoneInfo\n\nclass Cache:\n    def get(self, *args, **kwargs):\n        return None\n    def setdefault(self, *args, **kwargs):\n        return None\n    def clear(self, *args, **kwargs):\n        pass\n\nclass BombDescriptor:\n    def __get__(self, obj, owner):\n        return Cache()\n\nclass EvilZoneInfo(ZoneInfo):\n    pass\n\nEvilZoneInfo._weak_cache = BombDescriptor()\n\nEvilZoneInfo(\"UTC\")\n```\n\n**Related Code Snippet**\n\n```\nstatic PyObject *\nzoneinfo_ZoneInfo_impl(PyTypeObject *type, PyObject *key)\n/*[clinic end generated code: output=95e61dab86bb95c3 input=ef73d7a83bf8790e]*/\n{\n    zoneinfo_state *state = zoneinfo_get_state_by_self(type);\n    PyObject *instance = zone_from_strong_cache(state, type, key); // Trigged __eq__ method\n    if (instance != NULL || PyErr_Occurred()) {\n        return instance;\n    }\n\n    PyObject *weak_cache = get_weak_cache(state, type);\n    instance = PyObject_CallMethod(weak_cache, \"get\", \"O\", key, Py_None);\n    if (instance == NULL) {\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    if (instance == Py_None) {\n        Py_DECREF(instance);\n        PyObject *tmp = zoneinfo_new_instance(state, type, key);\n        if (tmp == NULL) {\n            return NULL;\n        }\n\n        instance =\n            PyObject_CallMethod(weak_cache, \"setdefault\", \"OO\", key, tmp);\n        Py_DECREF(tmp);\n        if (instance == NULL) {\n            return NULL;\n        }\n        ((PyZoneInfo_ZoneInfo *)instance)-\u003esource = SOURCE_CACHE;\n    }\n\n    update_strong_cache(state, type, key, instance);\n    return instance;\n}\n\nstatic PyObject *\nget_weak_cache(zoneinfo_state *state, PyTypeObject *type)\n{\n    if (type == state-\u003eZoneInfoType) {\n        return state-\u003eZONEINFO_WEAK_CACHE;\n    }\n    else {\n        PyObject *cache =\n            PyObject_GetAttrString((PyObject *)type, \"_weak_cache\");\n        \n        // BUG: The following DECREF free the newly assign cache and leads to UAF\n        // We are assuming that the type lives at least as long as the function\n        // that calls get_weak_cache, and that it holds a reference to the\n        // cache, so we'll return a \"borrowed reference\".\n        Py_XDECREF(cache);\n        return cache;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Affected Versions:**\n| Python Version | Status | Exit Code |\n|---|---|---|\n| `Python 3.9.24+ (heads/3.9:9c4638d, Oct 17 2025,             To see all available qualifiers, see our <a class="Link--inTextBlock" href="https://docs.github.com/search-github/github-code-search/understanding-github-code-search-syntax">documentation</a>.
          </p>
</form>        </div>

    </custom-scopes>

  <script type="application/json" data-target="react-app.embeddedData">{"payload":{"preloaded_records":{},"structured_data":{"@context":"https://schema.org","@type":"DiscussionForumPosting","headline":"Use-after-free in `zoneinfo.get_weak_cache` via weak DECREF assumption","articleBody":"### What happened?\n\n`get_weak_cache()` assumes that `_weak_cache` is always owned by the object and safe to DECREF. When _weak_cache is a descriptor returning a new object, this assumption breaks, causing the cache object to be freed too early and leading to a use-after-free in `zoneinfo_ZoneInfo_impl()`.\n\n**Proof of Concept:**\n```python\nfrom zoneinfo import ZoneInfo\n\nclass Cache:\n    def get(self, *args, **kwargs):\n        return None\n    def setdefault(self, *args, **kwargs):\n        return None\n    def clear(self, *args, **kwargs):\n        pass\n\nclass BombDescriptor:\n    def __get__(self, obj, owner):\n        return Cache()\n\nclass EvilZoneInfo(ZoneInfo):\n    pass\n\nEvilZoneInfo._weak_cache = BombDescriptor()\n\nEvilZoneInfo(\"UTC\")\n```\n\n**Related Code Snippet**\n\n```\nstatic PyObject *\nzoneinfo_ZoneInfo_impl(PyTypeObject *type, PyObject *key)\n/*[clinic end generated code: output=95e61dab86bb95c3 input=ef73d7a83bf8790e]*/\n{\n    zoneinfo_state *state = zoneinfo_get_state_by_self(type);\n    PyObject *instance = zone_from_strong_cache(state, type, key); // Trigged __eq__ method\n    if (instance != NULL || PyErr_Occurred()) {\n        return instance;\n    }\n\n    PyObject *weak_cache = get_weak_cache(state, type);\n    instance = PyObject_CallMethod(weak_cache, \"get\", \"O\", key, Py_None);\n    if (instance == NULL) {\n        return What happened?\n\n`get_weak_cache()` assumes that `_weak_cache` is always owned by the object and safe to DECREF. When _weak_cache is a descriptor returning a new object, this assumption breaks, causing the cache object to be freed too early and leading to a use-after-free in `zoneinfo_ZoneInfo_impl()`.\n\n**Proof of Concept:**\n```python\nfrom zoneinfo import ZoneInfo\n\nclass Cache:\n    def get(self, *args, **kwargs):\n        return None\n    def setdefault(self, *args, **kwargs):\n        return None\n    def clear(self, *args, **kwargs):\n        pass\n\nclass BombDescriptor:\n    def __get__(self, obj, owner):\n        return Cache()\n\nclass EvilZoneInfo(ZoneInfo):\n    pass\n\nEvilZoneInfo._weak_cache = BombDescriptor()\n\nEvilZoneInfo(\"UTC\")\n```\n\n**Related Code Snippet**\n\n```\nstatic PyObject *\nzoneinfo_ZoneInfo_impl(PyTypeObject *type, PyObject *key)\n/*[clinic end generated code: output=95e61dab86bb95c3 input=ef73d7a83bf8790e]*/\n{\n    zoneinfo_state *state = zoneinfo_get_state_by_self(type);\n    PyObject *instance = zone_from_strong_cache(state, type, key); // Trigged __eq__ method\n    if (instance != NULL || PyErr_Occurred()) {\n        return instance;\n    }\n\n    PyObject *weak_cache = get_weak_cache(state, type);\n    instance = PyObject_CallMethod(weak_cache, \"get\", \"O\", key, Py_None);\n    if (instance == NULL) {\n        return NULL;\n    }\n\n    if (instance == Py_None) {\n        Py_DECREF(instance);\n        PyObject *tmp = zoneinfo_new_instance(state, type, key);\n        if (tmp == NULL) {\n            return NULL;\n        }\n\n        instance =\n            PyObject_CallMethod(weak_cache, \"setdefault\", \"OO\", key, tmp);\n        Py_DECREF(tmp);\n        if (instance == NULL) {\n            return NULL;\n        }\n        ((PyZoneInfo_ZoneInfo *)instance)-\u003esource = SOURCE_CACHE;\n    }\n\n    update_strong_cache(state, type, key, instance);\n    return instance;\n}\n\nstatic PyObject *\nget_weak_cache(zoneinfo_state *state, PyTypeObject *type)\n{\n    if (type == state-\u003eZoneInfoType) {\n        return state-\u003eZONEINFO_WEAK_CACHE;\n    }\n    else {\n        PyObject *cache =\n            PyObject_GetAttrString((PyObject *)type, \"_weak_cache\");\n        \n        // BUG: The following DECREF free the newly assign cache and leads to UAF\n        // We are assuming that the type lives at least as long as the function\n        // that calls get_weak_cache, and that it holds a reference to the\n        // cache, so we'll return a \"borrowed reference\".\n        Py_XDECREF(cache);\n        return cache;\n    }\n}\n```\n\n**Affected Versions:**\n| Python Version | Status | Exit Code |\n|---|---|---|\n| `Python 3.9.24+ (heads/3.9:9c4638d, Oct 17 2025, vulnerability was in the get_weak_cache() function at Modules/_zoneinfo.c:303. The function incorrectly assumed that PyObject_GetAttrString() always returned a borrowed reference that could be immediately decremented with Py_XDECREF(). When _weak_cache was a descriptor (like the BombDescriptor in the PoC) that creates a new object each time it's accessed, this caused the newly created object to be freed too early, leading to use-after-free.\n\npossible fix method\n\n```c\nstatic PyObject *get_weak_cache(zoneinfo_state *state, PyTypeObject *type)\n{\n      if (type == state-\u003eZoneInfoType) {\n          Py_INCREF(state-\u003eZONEINFO_WEAK_CACHE);\n          return state-\u003eZONEINFO_WEAK_CACHE;\n      }\n      else {\n          return PyObject_GetAttrString((PyObject *)type, \"_weak_cache\");\n      }\n}\n```\n\nand call `Py_DECREF(weak_cache);` in callee","bodyHTML":"\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003eThe vulnerability was in the get_weak_cache() function at Modules/_zoneinfo.c:303. The function incorrectly assumed that PyObject_GetAttrString() always returned a borrowed reference that could be immediately decremented with Py_XDECREF(). When _weak_cache was a descriptor (like the BombDescriptor in the PoC) that creates a new object each time it's accessed, this caused the newly created object to be freed too early, leading to use-after-free.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp dir=\"auto\"\u003epossible fix method\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cdiv class=\"highlight highlight-source-c notranslate position-relative overflow-auto\" dir=\"auto\" class="ActivityHeader-module__narrowViewportWrapper__n_VAC IssueBodyHeader-module__narrowViewportWrapper__iLs_y"><div class="IssueBodyHeader-module__titleSection__dX9cz"><a class="ActivityHeader-module__narrowViewportWrapper__n_VAC IssueBodyHeader-module__actionsWrapper__D4Syp"><div class="ActivityHeader-module__edits__pnYtu IssueBodyHeader-module__editsSection__nQnXE"></div><div class="IssueBodyHeader-module__badgesSection___PWtJ"><div class="IssueBodyHeader-module__badgeGroup__EPYnd"></div><div class="IssueBodyHeader-module__actionsSection__gnoaX"><button data-component="IconButton" type="button" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false" tabindex="0" class="prc-Button-ButtonBase-9n-Xk prc-Button-IconButton-fyge7" data-loading="false" data-no-visuals="true" data-size="small" data-variant="invisible" aria-labelledby="_R_v5bd2mtb_" id="_R_15bd2mtb_"><svg data-component="Octicon" aria-hidden="true" focusable="false" class="octicon octicon-kebab-horizontal" viewBox="0 0 16 16" width="16" height="16" fill="currentColor" display="inline-block" overflow="visible" style="vertical-align:text-bottom"><path d="M8 9a1.5 1.5 0 1 0 0-3 1.5 1.5 0 0 0 0 3ZM1.5 9a1.5 1.5 0 1 0 0-3 1.5 1.5 0 0 0 0 3Zm13 0a1.5 1.5 0 1 0 0-3 1.5 1.5 0 0 0 0 3Z"></path></svg></button><span class="prc-TooltipV2-Tooltip-tLeuB" data-direction="s" data-component="Tooltip" aria-hidden="true" id="_R_v5bd2mtb_">Issue body actions</span></div></div></div></div></div><div class="IssueBodyViewer-module__IssueBody__xbjV0" id="issue-body-viewer" data-testid="issue-body-viewer"><div data-testid="markdown-body" data-team-hovercards-enabled="true" class="markdown-body" data-turbolinks="false"><div class="markdown-body NewMarkdownViewer-module__safe-html-box__ZT1eD"><h3 dir="auto">What happened?</h3>
<p dir="auto"><code class="notranslate">get_weak_cache()</code> assumes that <code class="notranslate">_weak_cache</code> is always owned by the object and safe to DECREF. When _weak_cache is a descriptor returning a new object, this assumption breaks, causing the cache object to be freed too early and leading to a use-after-free in <code class="notranslate">zoneinfo_ZoneInfo_impl()</code>.</p>
<p dir="auto"><strong>Proof of Concept:</strong></p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-python notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" dir="auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="from zoneinfo import ZoneInfo

class Cache:
    def get(self, *args, **kwargs):
        return None
    def setdefault(self, *args, **kwargs):
        return None
    def clear(self, *args, **kwargs):
        pass

class BombDescriptor:
    def __get__(self, obj, owner):
        return Cache()

class EvilZoneInfo(ZoneInfo):
    pass

EvilZoneInfo._weak_cache = BombDescriptor()

EvilZoneInfo(&quot;UTC&quot;)"><pre class="notranslate"><span class="pl-k">from</span> <span class="pl-s1">zoneinfo</span> <span class="pl-k">import</span> <span class="pl-v">ZoneInfo</span>

<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">Cache</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">get</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>, <span class="pl-c1">**</span><span class="pl-s1">kwargs</span>):
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">setdefault</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>, <span class="pl-c1">**</span><span class="pl-s1">kwargs</span>):
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-c1">None</span>
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">clear</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-c1">*</span><span class="pl-s1">args</span>, <span class="pl-c1">**</span><span class="pl-s1">kwargs</span>):
        <span class="pl-k">pass</span>

<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">BombDescriptor</span>:
    <span class="pl-k">def</span> <span class="pl-en">__get__</span>(<span class="pl-s1">self</span>, <span class="pl-s1">obj</span>, <span class="pl-s1">owner</span>):
        <span class="pl-k">return</span> <span class="pl-en">Cache</span>()

<span class="pl-k">class</span> <span class="pl-v">EvilZoneInfo</span>(<span class="pl-v">ZoneInfo</span>):
    <span class="pl-k">pass</span>

<span class="pl-v">EvilZoneInfo</span>.<span class="pl-c1">_weak_cache</span> <span class="pl-c1">=</span> <span class="pl-en">BombDescriptor</span>()

<p dir="auto"><strong>Related Code Snippet</strong></p>
<div class="snippet-clipboard-content notranslate position-relative overflow-auto" data-snippet-clipboard-copy-content="static PyObject *
zoneinfo_ZoneInfo_impl(PyTypeObject *type, PyObject *key)
/*[clinic end generated code: output=95e61dab86bb95c3 input=ef73d7a83bf8790e]*/
{
    zoneinfo_state *state = zoneinfo_get_state_by_self(type);
    PyObject *instance = zone_from_strong_cache(state, type, key); // Trigged __eq__ method
    if (instance != NULL || PyErr_Occurred()) {
        return instance;
    }

    PyObject *weak_cache = get_weak_cache(state, type);
    instance = PyObject_CallMethod(weak_cache, &quot;get&quot;, &quot;O&quot;, key, Py_None);
    if (instance == NULL) {
        return NULL;
    }

    if (instance == Py_None) {
        Py_DECREF(instance);
        PyObject *tmp = zoneinfo_new_instance(state, type, key);
        if (tmp == NULL) {
            return NULL;
        }

        instance =
            PyObject_CallMethod(weak_cache, &quot;setdefault&quot;, &quot;OO&quot;, key, tmp);
        Py_DECREF(tmp);
        if (instance == NULL) {
            return NULL;
        }
        ((PyZoneInfo_ZoneInfo *)instance)-&gt;source = SOURCE_CACHE;
    }

    update_strong_cache(state, type, key, instance);
    return instance;
}

static PyObject *
get_weak_cache(zoneinfo_state *state, PyTypeObject *type)
{
    if (type == state-&gt;ZoneInfoType) {
        return state-&gt;ZONEINFO_WEAK_CACHE;
    }
    else {
        PyObject *cache =
            PyObject_GetAttrString((PyObject *)type, &quot;_weak_cache&quot;);
        
        // BUG: The following DECREF free the newly assign cache and leads to UAF
        // We are assuming that the type lives at least as long as the function
        // that calls get_weak_cache, and that it holds a reference to the
        // cache, so we'll return a &quot;borrowed reference&quot;.
        Py_XDECREF(cache);
        return cache;
    }
}"><pre class="notranslate"><code class="notranslate">static PyObject *
zoneinfo_ZoneInfo_impl(PyTypeObject *type, PyObject *key)
/*[clinic end generated code: output=95e61dab86bb95c3 input=ef73d7a83bf8790e]*/
{
    zoneinfo_state *state = zoneinfo_get_state_by_self(type);
    PyObject *instance = zone_from_strong_cache(state, type, key); // Trigged __eq__ method
    if (instance != NULL || PyErr_Occurred()) {
        return instance;
    }

    PyObject *weak_cache = get_weak_cache(state, type);
    instance = PyObject_CallMethod(weak_cache, "get", "O", key, Py_None);
    if (instance == NULL) {
        return NULL;
    }

    if (instance == Py_None) {
        Py_DECREF(instance);
        PyObject *tmp = zoneinfo_new_instance(state, type, key);
        if (tmp == NULL) {
            return NULL;
        }

        instance =
            PyObject_CallMethod(weak_cache, "setdefault", "OO", key, tmp);
        Py_DECREF(tmp);
        if (instance == NULL) {
            return NULL;
        }
        ((PyZoneInfo_ZoneInfo *)instance)-&gt;source = SOURCE_CACHE;
    }

    update_strong_cache(state, type, key, instance);
    return instance;
}

static PyObject *
get_weak_cache(zoneinfo_state *state, PyTypeObject *type)
{
    if (type == state-&gt;ZoneInfoType) {
        return state-&gt;ZONEINFO_WEAK_CACHE;
    }
    else {
        PyObject *cache =
            PyObject_GetAttrString((PyObject *)type, "_weak_cache");
        
        // BUG: The following DECREF free the newly assign cache and leads to UAF
        // We are assuming that the type lives at least as long as the function
        // that calls get_weak_cache, and that it holds a reference to the
        // cache, so we'll return a "borrowed reference".
        Py_XDECREF(cache);
        return cache;
    }
}
</code></pre></div>
